## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population P and time t, which is the fundamental setup of population dynamics differential equations. The relationship likely captures density-dependent growth with possible time-varying effects.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Malthusian growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (exponential growth, density-independent)
- Logistic growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Allee effect model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (strong Allee effect with minimum viable population)
- Theta-logistic model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Richards growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**(c2)) (flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (growth with contest competition)
- Time-modulated logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal variation in growth)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic density dependence)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional power growth kinetics)
- Delayed density effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * P) (exponential density regulation)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P / (P + c3) (logistic growth with saturating harvest)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear proportionality to P â†’ density-independent (Malthusian) growth component: c0 * P
- Quadratic term PÂ² with negative coefficient â†’ intraspecific competition / density-dependent mortality
- Product P*(1 - c*P) â†’ logistic-type self-limiting growth with carrying capacity K = 1/c
- Logarithmic coupling log(P) multiplied by P â†’ Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate declines logarithmically
- Cubic terms PÂ³ or P*(P-a)*(K-P) â†’ Allee effect or bistability in population dynamics
- Exponential function of P, exp(-c*P) â†’ strong density regulation / overcrowding suppression
- Periodic functions of time sin(c*t), cos(c*t) â†’ seasonal or cyclic environmental forcing
- Ratio P/(P+c) â†’ saturating functional response (Type II) in predation or resource limitation
- Difference of power laws P^a - P^b â†’ balance between growth (anabolism) and loss (catabolism) processes
- Per-capita rate dP_dt/P being a decreasing function of P â†’ negative density dependence, fundamental ecological constraint
